cmake3-doc in EPEL 7

This page displays detailed information for a specific version of cmake3-doc. You might want go back to the main page of cmake3-doc.

Changelog

Date Author Change
2020-12-09 Antonio Trande - 3.17.5-1 - Release 3.17.5
2020-07-19 Neal Gompa - 3.17.3-3 - Backport support for out-of-source builds controlled by __cmake3_in_source_build macro - Backport cmake3_build and cmake3_install macros - Backport ctest3 macro
2020-06-11 Antonio Trande - 3.17.3-2 - Change command to add Python shebang of the cmake3.prov file (epel bz#1845614)
2020-06-01 Antonio Trande - 3.17.3-1 - Release 3.17.3
2020-04-29 Antonio Trande - 3.17.2-1 - Release 3.17.2
2020-04-27 Antonio Trande - 3.17.1-2 - Fix macros for bundled libraries - Add Provides for bundled libraries
2020-04-26 Antonio Trande - 3.17.1-1 - Release 3.17.1 - Drop EPEL6 support - Add openssl BR - Fix rhbz#1811358 - Use system zstd
2020-03-08 Antonio Trande - 3.14.7-1 - Bugfix release 3.14.7
2019-09-01 Antonio Trande - 3.14.6-2 - Fix rename patches
2019-08-27 Antonio Trande - 3.14.6-1 - Update to cmake-3.14.6 (rhbz#1746146, rhbz#1746104) - Do not use system jsoncpp - Split off appdata file as external source file
